<td style="width:11%;vertical-align:top"><span style="font-weight:bold">Item&#160;1.01.</span></td>
<td style="vertical-align:top"> <p style=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;text-align:left">Entry into a Material Definitive Agreement.</p></td></tr></table> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On November&#160;20, 2020, Tilray, Inc. (&#8220;Tilray&#8221;) entered into privately negotiated exchange agreements (the &#8220;Exchange Agreements&#8221;) with certain holders of Tilray&#8217;s 5.00% Convertible Senior Notes due 2023 (the &#8220;Notes&#8221;). Under the terms of the Exchange Agreements, the holders agreed to exchange an aggregate principal amount of approximately $124.3&#160;million of Notes plus accrued interest held by them in exchange for an aggregate of 10,932,222 shares of Tilray&#8217;s Class&#160;2 common stock (&#8220;Shares&#8221;). Effectively, Tilray agreed to repurchase a portion of its Notes at a 36% discount to their face value, using shares issued at Tilray&#8217;s most recent closing market price on November&#160;20, 2020 (which is equivalent to a conversion price of $7.36 per share). These exchange transactions closed on November 24, 2020.</p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On November 23, 2020, Tilray entered into additional Exchange Agreements with certain holders of the Notes. Under the terms of the Exchange Agreements, the holders agreed to exchange an aggregate principal amount of approximately $72.9 million of Notes plus accrued interest held by them in exchange for an aggregate of 6,407,355 shares. Effectively, Tilray agreed to repurchase a portion of its Notes at a 42% discount to their face value, using shares issued at Tilray&#8217;s most recent closing market price on November 23, 2020 (which is equivalent to a conversion price of $6.68 per share). These exchange transactions are expected to close on or about November 25, 2020, subject to customary closing conditions.</p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Immediately following the exchange of the Notes contemplated by the Exchange Agreements, approximately $277.9&#160;million in aggregate principal amount of the Notes will remain outstanding.</p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The foregoing description of the Exchange Agreements is qualified in its entirety by reference to the form of Exchange Agreement attached as Exhibit&#160;99.1 hereto.</p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On November 23, 2020 and November 24, 2020, Tilray issued press releases announcing the Exchange Agreements, copies of which are attached hereto as Exhibit 99.2 and 99.3, respectively, and incorporated herein by reference.</p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">This Current Report does not constitute an offer to sell, or a solicitation of an offer to buy, any security and shall not constitute an offer, solicitation or sale in any jurisdiction in which such offering would be unlawful.</p> <p style="font-size:18pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&#160;</p>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right"><B>Exhibit 99.1 </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:16pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>Form of Exchange Agreement </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right">November&nbsp;[&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;], 2020 </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Tilray, Inc. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">1100 Maughan Rd. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Nanaimo, BC, Canada V9X 1J2 </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">Re:</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Exchange of 5.00% Convertible Senior Notes due 2023 for Class&nbsp;2 Common Stock </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:14pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Ladies and Gentlemen: </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">This Exchange Agreement and the Terms
and Conditions for Exchange of Securities, attached hereto as <U>Exhibit</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;A</U> (the &#147;<B>Terms and Conditions</B>&#148; and, together with this Exchange Agreement, the &#147;<B>Agreement</B>&#148;), is made as of the date
hereof between Tilray,&nbsp;Inc. (the &#147;<B>Company</B>&#148;) and the Investor (as&nbsp;defined below). </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">WHEREAS, the Company and the Investor desire
to exchange (the &#147;<B>Exchange</B>&#148;) certain 5.00% Convertible Senior Notes due 2023, CUSIP 88688T AB6 (the &#147;<B>Notes</B>&#148;) issued by the Company and held by the Investor for shares of the Company&#146;s Class&nbsp;2 Common Stock,
par value $0.0001 per share (the &#147;<B>Common Stock</B>&#148;); and </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">WHEREAS, the Company desires to repurchase from each Exchanging Investor, and each
Exchanging Investors desire to sell to the Company, the Notes for a purchase price equal to [&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;]% of the principal amount thereof plus accrued and unpaid interest and in respect thereof, the Company desires to issue to each
Exchanging Investor, Shares (as defined below) valued at $[&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;] per share based on the Company&#146;s closing stock price on The Nasdaq Global Select Market on November&nbsp;[&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;],
2020. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The undersigned investor (the &#147;<B>Investor</B>&#148;), for itself and on behalf of the beneficial owners listed on
<U>Exhibit</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;B.1</U> hereto (&#147;<B>Accounts</B>&#148;) for whom the Investor holds contractual and investment authority (each, including the Investor if it is a party exchanging Notes, an &#147;<B>Exchanging Investor</B>&#148;),
hereby agrees to exchange, with Tilray,&nbsp;Inc. (the &#147;<B>Company</B>&#148;), certain Notes for shares of the Company&#146;s Common Stock.&nbsp;The Investor understands that the Exchange is being made without registration of the offer or sale
of the Shares under the Securities Act of 1933, as amended (the &#147;<B>Securities Act</B>&#148;), or any securities laws of any state of the United States or of any other jurisdiction and that the Shares are being offered only to institutional
&#147;accredited investors&#148; within the meaning of Rule&nbsp;501 of Regulation D under the Securities Act that are also &#147;qualified institutional buyers&#148; within the meaning of Rule&nbsp;144A under the Securities Act, pursuant to a
private placement exemption from registration under Section&nbsp;4(a)(2)&nbsp;of the Securities Act. The Company intends for the shares of Common Stock to be issued in the Exchange will not be &#147;restricted securities&#148; under Rule 144 under
the Securities Act. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Subject to the terms and conditions of this Agreement, the Investor hereby agrees to exchange, and cause the other Exchanging
Investors to exchange, an aggregate principal amount of the Notes set forth on <U>Exhibit B.1</U> hereto (the &#147;<B>Exchanged Notes</B>&#148;) for (a)&nbsp;a number of shares per $1,000 principal amount of such Exchanged Notes equal to the
product of [&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;]% of $1,000 divided by $[&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;] (such number of shares of Common Stock in respect of all Exchanged Notes for each Exchanging Investor, the &#147;<B>Exchange</B>
<B>Shares</B>&#148;) and (b)&nbsp;a number of shares of Common Stock in respect of accrued and unpaid interest equal to the product of accrued and unpaid interest on the Exchanged Notes to, but excluding, the Closing Date (as defined below), divided
by $[&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;] (the &#147;<B>Accrued</B> <B>Interest Shares</B>&#148; and, together with the Exchange Shares, the &#147;<B>Shares</B>&#148;), and the Company agrees to deliver the Shares on the Closing Date to
each Exchanging Investor in exchange for such Exchanged Notes. </P>
</DIV></Center>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">At or prior to the times set forth in <U>Exhibit</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;B.2</U> hereto (the &#147;<B>Exchange
Procedures</B>&#148;), the Investor shall cause the Exchanged Notes to be delivered by book entry transfer through the facilities of The Depository Trust Company (&#147;<B>DTC</B>&#148;) to GLAS Trust Company LLC, in its capacity as trustee of the
Notes (in such capacity, the &#147;<B>Trustee</B>&#148;), for the account/benefit of the Company for cancellation as instructed in the Exchange Procedures and on the Closing Date, subject to satisfaction of the conditions precedent specified in
Section&nbsp;5 of the Terms and Conditions and the prior receipt by the Trustee from the Investor of the Exchanged Notes, the Company shall deliver the Shares to the DTC account to the account specified by the Investor for each relevant Exchanging
Investor in <U>Exhibit</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;B.1</U> as set forth in the Terms and Conditions.</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Subject to the terms and conditions of this Agreement, the
Investor hereby, for itself and on behalf of its Accounts, (a)&nbsp;waives any and all other rights with respect to such Exchanged Notes and (b)&nbsp;releases and discharges the Company from any and all claims the undersigned and its Accounts may
now have, or may have in the future, arising out of, or related to, such Exchanged Notes. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Each of the provisions of the Terms and Conditions is
incorporated herein by reference in its entirety, and shall be deemed to be a part of this Exchange Agreement to the same extent as if such provisions had been set forth in full herein; and each of the representations, warranties, and agreements set
forth therein shall be deemed to have been made at and as of the date of this Exchange Agreement.&nbsp;Unless otherwise defined herein, terms defined in the Terms and Conditions are used herein as therein defined. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">This Agreement constitutes the entire agreement between the Company and the Investor with respect to the subject matters hereof. This Exchange Agreement may
be executed by one or more of the parties hereto in any number of separate counterparts (including by facsimile or other electronic means, including telecopy, email or otherwise), and all of said counterparts taken together shall be deemed to
constitute one and the same instrument.&nbsp;Delivery of an executed signature page&nbsp;of this Exchange Agreement by facsimile or other transmission (<I>e.g.</I>, &#147;pdf&#148; or &#147;tif&#148; format) shall be effective as delivery of a
manually executed counterpart hereof. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">[SIGNATURE PAGE FOLLOWS] </P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:16pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B><U>Terms and Conditions for Exchange of Securities </U></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:14pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Each of Tilray,&nbsp;Inc. a Delaware corporation (the &#147;<B>Company</B>&#148;), and the undersigned (the &#147;<B>Investor</B>&#148;), for
itself and on behalf of the beneficial owners listed on <U>Exhibit</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;B.1</U> to the Exchange Agreement for whom the Investor holds contractual and investment authority (together with the Investor, the &#147;<B>Exchanging
Investors</B>&#148;), hereby confirms its agreement pursuant to that certain exchange agreement, dated as of the date hereof (the &#147;<B>Exchange Agreement</B>&#148;), to which these Terms and Conditions for Exchange of Securities (the
&#147;<B>Terms and Conditions</B>&#148;) are attached as <U>Exhibit</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;A</U>, as set forth in these Terms and Conditions and in the Exchange Agreement (together, this &#147;<B>Agreement</B>&#148;) relating to the exchange of the
Exchanged Notes for the Shares as set forth in this Agreement.&nbsp;Capitalized terms used but not defined in the Terms and Conditions have the meanings set forth in the Exchange Agreement. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">1.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <U>Exchange Consideration; Exchange</U>.&nbsp;On the basis of the representations, warranties and agreements herein contained and
subject to the terms and conditions herein set forth, the Investor hereby agrees to exchange, and to cause the other Exchanging Investors to exchange an aggregate principal amount of the Notes set forth on <U>Exhibit B.1</U> to the Exchange
Agreement (the &#147;<B>Exchanged Notes</B>&#148;) for the Shares, as set forth on <U>Exhibit B.1</U> to the Exchange Agreement. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">For the
avoidance of doubt, no cash will be paid to any Exchanging Investor in respect of fractional shares. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Exchange shall occur in
accordance with the Exchange Procedures; <U>provided</U> that each of the Company and the Investor acknowledges that the delivery of the Exchanged Notes for withdrawal through the Deposits and Withdrawal at Custodian (&#147;<B>DWAC</B>&#148;)
program through the DTC or the delivery of the Shares to any Exchanging Investor may be delayed due to procedures and mechanics within the system of the DTC or The Nasdaq Global Select Market (&#147;<B>NASDAQ</B>&#148;) (including the procedures and
mechanics regarding the listing of the Shares on NASDAQ) and that such a delay will not be a default under this Agreement so long as (i)&nbsp;the Investor and/or the Company, as the case may be, is using its reasonable best efforts to effect such
delivery, and (ii)&nbsp;such delay is no longer than three business days; <U>provided</U>, <U>further</U>, that no delivery of Shares will be made until such Exchanged Notes have been properly submitted for withdrawal through the DWAC program in
accordance with this Agreement, and no accrued interest will be payable by reason of any delay in making such delivery; <U>provided</U>, <U>further</U>, that for the avoidance of doubt, the Company shall deliver the Shares upon confirmation by the
Investor to the Company that it has submitted the DWAC withdrawal for the Exchanged Notes. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The cancellation of the Exchanged Notes shall
be effected through the DWAC program in accordance with the customary procedures of the Trustee. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">2.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <U>The Closing</U>. The

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right"><B><U>EXHIBIT&nbsp;B.2 </U></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">Exchange Procedures </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:16pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B><U>NOTICE
TO INVESTOR </U></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:14pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Attached are Investor Exchange Procedures for the settlement of the exchange of 5.00% Convertible Senior Notes due
2023, CUSIP&nbsp;88688T AB6 (the &#147;<B>Notes</B>&#148;) of Tilray,&nbsp;Inc. (the &#147;<B>Company</B>&#148;) for shares of the Company&#146;s common stock, par value $0.0001 per share (the&nbsp;&#147;<B>Shares</B>&#148;) pursuant to the Exchange
Agreement, dated as of November&nbsp;[&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;], 2020, between you and the Company which is expected to on or about November&nbsp;[&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;], 2020.&nbsp;To ensure timely settlement, please follow the instructions for
exchanging your Notes for Shares as set forth on the following page. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">These instructions supersede any prior instructions you
received.&nbsp;Your failure to comply with the attached instructions may delay your receipt of Shares for your Notes. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">If you have any
questions, please contact Iain Franks of Cowen and Company, LLC at iain.franks@cowen.com or (415) <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">646-7266.</FONT> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Thank you. </P>
</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Delivery of Notes </U></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:8pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">You must direct the eligible DTC participant through which you hold a beneficial interest in the Notes to post <B>on
November</B><B></B><B>&nbsp;[&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;], 2020, no later than&nbsp;9:00 a.m., New York City time</B>, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">one-sided</FONT> withdrawal instructions through DTC via DWAC for the aggregate principal amount of
Notes (CUSIP/ISIN&nbsp;#&nbsp;88688T AB6 / US88688TAB61) set forth in Exhibit&nbsp;B.1 of the Exchange Agreement to be exchanged for Shares.&nbsp;<B>It is important that this instruction be submitted and the
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">one-sided</FONT> DWAC withdrawal (not a deliver vs. payment or free delivery) is posted on November</B><B></B><B>&nbsp;[&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;], 2020</B>. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>To receive Shares: </U></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:8pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">You must direct your eligible DTC
participant through which you wish to hold a beneficial interest in the Shares to be issued upon exchange to post <B>no later than 9:00 a.m., New York City time</B>, <B>on November</B><B></B><B>&nbsp;[&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;], 2020</B>, a <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">one-sided</FONT> deposit instruction through DTC via DWAC for a number of Shares deliverable in respect of the Exchanged Notes.&nbsp;<B>It is important that this instruction be submitted and the DWAC posted on
November</B><B></B><B>&nbsp;[&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;], 2020</B>. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Closing </U></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:8pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On November&nbsp;[&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;], 2020, after the Company receives your delivery instructions as set forth above and a withdrawal request in respect
of the Exchanged Notes has been posted as specified above, and subject to the satisfaction of the conditions to Closing as set forth in your Exchange Agreement, the Company will deliver your Shares in respect of your Notes exchanged in accordance
with the delivery instructions above. </P>
</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right"><B><U>EXHIBIT&nbsp;C </U></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:14pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Under U.S. federal income tax law, a holder who exchanges Notes for Shares generally must provide such holder&#146;s correct TIN on IRS <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Form&nbsp;W-9</FONT> below or otherwise establish a basis for exemption from backup withholding. A TIN is generally an individual holder&#146;s social security number or a holder&#146;s employer identification number. If
the correct TIN is not provided, the holder may be subject to a $50 penalty imposed by the IRS under Section&nbsp;6723 of the Internal Revenue Code of 1986, as amended. In addition, certain payments made to holders may be subject to U.S. backup
withholding (currently set at 28% of the payment). If a holder is required to provide a TIN but does not have a TIN, the holder should consult its tax advisor regarding how to obtain a TIN. Certain holders are not subject to these backup withholding
and reporting requirements. A <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-U.S.</FONT> holder must establish its status as an exempt recipient from backup withholding and can do so by submitting a properly completed IRS
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Form&nbsp;W-8</FONT> (available from the Company), signed, under penalties of perjury, attesting to such holder&#146;s exempt foreign status.&nbsp;U.S. backup withholding is not an additional tax. Rather, the U.S.
federal income tax liability of persons subject to backup withholding will be reduced by the amount of tax withheld. If withholding results in an overpayment of taxes, a refund may be obtained provided that the required information is timely
furnished to the IRS.&nbsp;Holders are urged to consult their tax advisors regarding how to complete the appropriate forms and to determine whether they are exempt from backup withholding or other withholding taxes. </P>
</DIV></Center>

<TABLE CELLSPACING="0" CELLPADDING="0" WIDTH="100%" BORDER="0" STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" ALIGN="center">

<TD VALIGN="bottom"><B>PRESS RELEASE</B></TD>

</TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="line-height:1.5pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:2pt;border-bottom:1.50pt solid #000000">&nbsp;</P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Tilray, Inc. Announces Agreement to Exchange Approximately $124.3 Million in Principal Amount of Its 5.00% Convertible Senior Notes Due 2023 for Common
Stock </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>NANAIMO, BRITISH COLUMBIA </B>&#150; Tilray,&nbsp;Inc. (&#147;Tilray&#148; or the &#147;Company&#148;) (Nasdaq: TLRY), a global pioneer in
cannabis research, cultivation, production and distribution, today announced that it has entered into a privately negotiated exchange agreement with a certain holder of its 5.00% Convertible Senior Notes due 2023 (the &#147;Notes&#148;). Pursuant to
the exchange agreement, the Company will exchange approximately $124.3&nbsp;million in aggregate principal amount of Notes plus accrued interest, for approximately 10.9&nbsp;million shares of the Company&#146;s Class&nbsp;2 common stock. The
exchange transaction is expected to be completed on or about November&nbsp;24, 2020, subject to customary closing conditions. Following the exchange transaction, approximately $350.7&nbsp;million in aggregate principal amount of the Notes will
remain outstanding. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Effectively, the Company agreed to repurchase a portion of its Notes at a 36% discount to their face value, using shares issued at
the Company&#146;s most recent closing market price (which is equivalent to a conversion price of $7.36 per share). </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The purpose of the transaction was to
reduce the Company&#146;s debt and eliminate $6.2&nbsp;million in annual cash interest costs. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The shares of the Company&#146;s Class&nbsp;2 common stock
issuable upon the exchange have not been registered under the Securities Act of 1933, as amended, or the securities laws of any state or other jurisdiction, and may not be offered or sold in the United States absent registration or an applicable
exemption from registration requirements. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">This press release does not constitute an offer to sell or a solicitation to buy any of the securities
described herein, nor shall there be any sale of these securities in any state or jurisdiction in which such offer, solicitation or sale would be unlawful. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt" ALIGN="center">

<TD VALIGN="top"><B>PRESS RELEASE</B></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD VALIGN="top" ALIGN="right"><B>November 24, 2020</B></TD></TR>
</TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="line-height:1.5pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:2pt;border-bottom:1.50pt solid #000000">&nbsp;</P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Tilray, Inc. Announces Agreement to Exchange an Additional $72.9 Million in Principal Amount of Its 5.00% Convertible Senior Notes Due 2023 for Common
Stock </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>NANAIMO, BRITISH COLUMBIA </B>&#150; Tilray,&nbsp;Inc. (&#147;Tilray&#148; or the &#147;Company&#148;) (Nasdaq: TLRY), a global pioneer in
cannabis research, cultivation, production and distribution, today announced that it has entered into privately negotiated exchange agreements with certain holders of its 5.00% Convertible Senior Notes due 2023 (the &#147;Notes&#148;). Pursuant to
the exchange agreements, the Company will exchange approximately $72.9&nbsp;million in aggregate principal amount of Notes plus accrued interest, for approximately 6.4&nbsp;million shares of the Company&#146;s Class&nbsp;2 common stock. The exchange
transactions are expected to be completed on or about November&nbsp;25, 2020, subject to customary closing conditions. Following the exchange transactions, approximately $277.9&nbsp;million in aggregate principal amount of the Notes will remain
outstanding. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Effectively, the Company agreed to repurchase a portion of its Notes at a 42% discount to their face value, using shares issued at the
Company&#146;s most recent closing market price (which is equivalent to a conversion price of $6.68 per share). </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The purpose of the transaction was to
reduce the Company&#146;s debt and eliminate approximately $3.6&nbsp;million in annual cash interest costs. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The shares of the Company&#146;s Class&nbsp;2
common stock issuable upon the exchanges have not been registered under the Securities Act of 1933, as amended, or the securities laws of any state or other jurisdiction, and may not be offered or sold in the United States absent registration or an
applicable exemption from registration requirements. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">This press release does not constitute an offer to sell or a solicitation to buy any of the
securities described herein, nor shall there be any sale of these securities in any state or jurisdiction in which such offer, solicitation or sale would be unlawful. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:36pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<P STYLE="font-size:36pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="font-size:36pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="font-size:36pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
